The note is either created from scratch with the powerful tools within the app or by importing files from PDF or Microsoft Office formats. Opening the Class Note starts a class. The students can write answers, sketch drawings or import photos and graphics to illustrate their ideas.  Teachers can monitor how each student or group is progressing through the lesson. Easy management controls even allow the teacher to pass presentation control to the student to demonstrate their work.\r\n\r\nFollowing the lesson presented in class, students can join collaborative study groups and work through their homework together by checking in to the same document and sharing ideas within it.
